-------------------BRF206_MAPPING_PROCEDURE---------

create or replace PROCEDURE "BRF206_MAPPING_PROCEDURE" (REPORT_DATE VARCHAR2) 

IS 
  V_REPORT_DATE DATE := To_date (REPORT_DATE, 'DD-MM-YYYY'); 
BEGIN


--INSERT VALUES
INSERT INTO  BRF206_MAPPING_TABLE(foracid,ACCT_NAME,REPORT_DATE,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE)
SELECT ACCT_NO ,ACCT_NAME,REPORT_DATE,CURRENCY FROM brf_treasury_master_tb where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE and
ACCT_NO IN ('A31013016','A31031210','A34022024','A34022200','A66044200');

INSERT INTO  BRF206_MAPPING_TABLE(foracid,ACCT_NAME,REPORT_DATE,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE)
SELECT ACCT_NO ,ACCT_NAME,REPORT_DATE,CURRENCY FROM brf_treasury_master_tb where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE and
ACCT_NO IN ('A33012100');
COMMIT;

----------------BRF206_DETAIL_PROCEDURE------------------


create or replace PROCEDURE BRF206_DETAIL_PROCEDURE (REPORT_DATE DATE)
IS
   v_report_date   date := to_date (report_date, 'DD-MM-YYYY');
BEGIN


delete from BRF206_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE;
Commit;


insert into BRF206_DETAILTABLE
( foracid,ACCT_NAME,REPORT_DATE, REPORT_LABEL_1,REPORT_NAME_1,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1)
SELECT  foracid,ACCT_NAME,REPORT_DATE,REPORT_LABEL_1,REPORT_NAME_1,ACCT_CRNCY_CODE,REPORT_ADDL_CRITERIA_1 FROM 
brf206_mapping_table where report_date = '30-jun-2023' AND REPORT_LABEL_1 IS NOT NULL ;


COMMIT;---RESIDENT


MERGE INTO BRF206_DETAILTABLE M
USING (
    SELECT distinct   b.REPORT_LABEL_1,b.cust_id,b.foracid
    FROM BRF206_MAPPING_TABLE b
    JOIN BRF206_DETAILTABLE a ON a.foracid = b.foracid
    WHERE a.report_date = V_REPORT_DATE
) S
ON (M.foracid = S.foracid)
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE
SET M.REPORT_LABEL_1 = S.REPORT_LABEL_1
WHERE M.report_date = V_REPORT_DATE;
COMMIT;

MERGE INTO BRF206_DETAILTABLE M
USING (
    SELECT distinct  b.nre_status,b.cust_id,b.foracid
    FROM BRF206_MAPPING_TABLE b
    JOIN BRF206_DETAILTABLE a ON a.foracid = b.foracid
    WHERE a.report_date = V_REPORT_DATE
) S
ON (M.foracid = S.foracid)
WHEN MATCHED THEN UPDATE
SET M.NRE_FLG = S.nre_status
WHERE M.report_date = V_REPORT_DATE;

    -- Commit outside the loop
    
    delete from BRF206_DETAILTABLE where report_date = V_REPORT_DATE and report_label_1 is null;
Commit;
    COMMIT;

END;
